It computes all possible forms of 2-time correlations (includes the previous 2op and reverse functionality) from the 3operator version. 2op correlations are computed by setting one of the three to the identity. - the new function works for me, es, and mc solvers. both me and mc work for time-dependent hamiltonians - still need to implement mc "steady state" (see doc string for what I plan to do) - the old api can be added back if necessary BUT 2op_1t is super misleading IMO so I think it should not be added back - I got quite confused over it.
